StableGen is designed to apply textures to \u003cstrong\u003eall mesh objects in your scene simultaneously\u003c/strong\u003e from your defined camera viewpoints. Alternatively, you can choose to texture only selected objects.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAchieve a cohesive look across entire environments or collections of assets in a single generation pass.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIdeal for concept art, look development for complex scenes, and batch-texturing asset libraries.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e \u003cstrong\u003eMulti-View Consistency:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSequential Mode:\u003c/strong\u003e Generates textures viewpoint by viewpoint on each mesh, using inpainting and visibility masks for high consistency across complex surfaces.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGrid Mode:\u003c/strong\u003e Processes multiple viewpoints for all meshes simultaneously for faster previews. Includes an optional refinement pass.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSophisticated weighted blending ensures smooth transitions between views.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e \u003cstrong\u003ePrecise Geometric Control with ControlNet:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eLeverage multiple ControlNet units (Depth, Canny, Normal) simultaneously to ensure generated textures respect your model's geometry.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFine-tune strength, start/end steps for each ControlNet unit.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports custom ControlNet model mapping.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e锔 \u003cstrong\u003ePowerful Style Guidance with IPAdapter:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUse external reference images to guide the style, mood, and content of your textures with IPAdapter.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEmploy IPAdapter without an reference image for enhanced consistency in multi-view generation modes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eControl IPAdapter strength, weight type, and active steps.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e锔 \u003cstrong\u003eFlexible ComfyUI Backend:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eConnects to your existing ComfyUI installation, allowing you to use your preferred SDXL checkpoints and custom LoRAs. Experimental support for FLUX.1-dev.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOffloads heavy computation to the ComfyUI server, keeping Blender mostly responsive.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e \u003cstrong\u003eAdvanced Inpainting \u0026amp; Refinement:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRefine Mode (Img2Img):\u003c/strong\u003e Re-style, enhance, or add detail to existing textures (StableGen generated or otherwise) using an image-to-image process. Choose to preserve original textures for localized refinement.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUV Inpaint Mode:\u003c/strong\u003e Intelligently fills untextured areas directly on your model's UV map using surrounding texture context.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e锔 \u003cstrong\u003eIntegrated Workflow Tools:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCamera Setup:\u003c/strong\u003e Quickly add and arrange multiple cameras around your subject.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eView-Specific Prompts:\u003c/strong\u003e Assign unique text prompts to individual camera viewpoints for targeted details.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTexture Baking:\u003c/strong\u003e Convert complex procedural StableGen materials into standard UV image textures.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHDRI Setup, Modifier Application, Curve Conversion, GIF/MP4 Export \u0026amp; Reproject.\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e \u003cstrong\u003ePreset System:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eGet started quickly with built-in presets for common scenarios (e.g., \"Default\", \"Characters\", \"Quick Draft\").\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSave and manage your own custom parameter configurations for repeatable workflows.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eStableGen acts as an intuitive interface within Blender that communicates with a ComfyUI backend.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eYou set up your scene and parameters in the StableGen panel.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eStableGen prepares necessary data (like ControlNet inputs from camera views).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIt constructs a workflow and sends it to your ComfyUI server.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eComfyUI processes the request using your selected diffusion models.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eGenerated images are sent back to Blender.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eStableGen applies these images as textures to your models using sophisticated projection and blending techniques.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" href=\"#-system-requirements\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 Prepare Scene:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHave a mesh object ready (e.g., the default Cube).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEnsure the StableGen addon is enabled and configured (see Step 4 above).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAccess StableGen Panel:\u003c/strong\u003e Press \u003ccode\u003eN\u003c/code\u003e in the 3D Viewport, go to the \"StableGen\" tab.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAdd Cameras (Recommended for Multi-View):\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSelect your object.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIn the StableGen panel, click \"\u003cstrong\u003eAdd Cameras\u003c/strong\u003e\". Choose \u003ccode\u003eObject\u003c/code\u003e as center type. Adjust interactively if needed, then confirm.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSet Basic Parameters:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePrompt:\u003c/strong\u003e Type a description (e.g., \"ancient stone wall with moss\").\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCheckpoint:\u003c/strong\u003e Select a checkpoint (e.g., \u003ccode\u003esdxl_base_1.0\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGeneration Mode:\u003c/strong\u003e \u003ccode\u003eSequential\u003c/code\u003e is a good starting point for consistency.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHit Generate!\u003c/strong\u003e Click the main \"\u003cstrong\u003eGenerate\u003c/strong\u003e\" button.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eObserve:\u003c/strong\u003e Watch the progress in the panel and the ComfyUI console. Your object should update with the new texture! Output files will be in your specified \"Output Directory\".\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBy default, the generated texture will only be visible in the Rendered viewport shading mode (CYCLES Render Engine).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e Usage \u0026amp; Parameters Overview\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content--usage--parameters-overview\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink:  Usage \u0026amp; Parameters Overview\" href=\"#-usage--parameters-overview\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eStableGen provides a comprehensive interface for controlling your AI texturing process, from initial setup to final output. Here's an overview of the main sections and tools available in the StableGen panel:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003ePrimary Actions \u0026amp; Scene Setup\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-primary-actions--scene-setup\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Primary Actions \u0026amp; Scene Setup\" href=\"#primary-actions--scene-setup\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThese are the main operational buttons and initial setup tools, generally found near the top of the StableGen panel:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGenerate / Cancel Generation (Main Button):\u003c/strong\u003e This is the primary button to start the AI texture generation process for meshe objects based on your current settings. It communicates with the ComfyUI backend. While processing, the button changes to \"Cancel Generation,\" allowing you to stop the current task. Progress bars will appear below this button during generation.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBake Textures:\u003c/strong\u003e Converts the dynamic, multi-projection material StableGen creates on your meshes into a single, standard UV-mapped image texture per object. This is essential for exporting or simplifying scenes. You can set the resolution and UV unwrapping method for the bake. This option is crucial for finalizing your AI-generated textures into a portable format.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAdd Cameras:\u003c/strong\u003e Helps you quickly set up multiple viewpoints. It creates a circular array of Blender cameras around the active object (if \"Object\" center type is chosen) or the current 3D view center. You can specify the number of cameras and interactively adjust their positions before finalizing.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCollect Camera Prompts:\u003c/strong\u003e Cycles through all cameras in your scene, allowing you to type a specific descriptive text prompt for each viewpoint (e.g., \"front view,\" \"close-up on face\"). These per-camera prompts are used in conjunction with the main prompt if \u003ccode\u003eUse camera prompts\u003c/code\u003e is enabled in \u003ccode\u003eViewpoint Blending Settings\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003ePreset system allows you to:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSelect a Preset:\u003c/strong\u003e Choose from built-in configurations (e.g., controls for defining the generation:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePrompt:\u003c/strong\u003e The main text description of the texture you want to generate.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCheckpoint:\u003c/strong\u003e Select the base SDXL checkpoint.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eArchitecture:\u003c/strong\u003e Choose between \u003ccode\u003eSDXL\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eFlux 1\u003c/code\u003e (experimental) model architectures.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGeneration Mode:\u003c/strong\u003e Defines the core strategy for texturing:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eGenerate Separately\u003c/code\u003e: Each viewpoint generates independently.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eGenerate Sequentially\u003c/code\u003e: Viewpoints generate one by one, using inpainting from previous views for consistency.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eGenerate Using Grid\u003c/code\u003e: Combines all views into a grid for a single generation pass, with an optional refinement step.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eRefine/Restyle Texture (Img2Img)\u003c/code\u003e: Uses the current texture as input for an image-to-image process.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eUV Inpaint Missing Areas\u003c/code\u003e: Fills untextured areas on a UV map via inpainting.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTarget Objects:\u003c/strong\u003e Choose whether to texture all visible mesh objects or only selected ones.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eAdvanced Parameters (Collapsible settings:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCore Generation Settings:\u003c/strong\u003e Control diffusion basics like Seed, Steps, CFG, Negative Prompt, Sampler, Scheduler and Clip Skip.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLoRA Management:\u003c/strong\u003e Add and configure LoRAs (Low-Rank Adaptation) for additional style or content guidance. You can set the model and clip strength for each LoRA.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eViewpoint Blending Settings:\u003c/strong\u003e Manage how textures from different camera views are combined, including camera-specific prompts, discard angles, and blending weight exponents.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOutput \u0026amp; Material Settings:\u003c/strong\u003e Define fallback color, material properties (BSDF), automatic resolution scaling, and options for baking textures during generation which enables generating with more than 8 viewpoints.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eImage Guidance (IPAdapter \u0026amp; ControlNet):\u003c/strong\u003e Configure IPAdapter for style transfer using external images and set up multiple ControlNet units (Depth, Canny, etc.) for precise structural control.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eInpainting Options:\u003c/strong\u003e Fine-tune masking and blending for \u003ccode\u003eSequential\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eUV Inpaint\u003c/code\u003e modes (e.g., differential diffusion, mask blurring/growing).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGeneration Mode Specifics:\u003c/strong\u003e Parameters unique to the selected Generation Mode, like refinement options for Grid mode or IPAdapter consistency settings for Sequential/Separate/Refine modes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eIntegrated Workflow Tools (Bottom Section)\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-integrated-workflow-tools-bottom-section\" class=\"anchor\" 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eA collection of utilities to further support your texturing workflow:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSwitch Material:\u003c/strong\u003e For selected objects with multiple material slots, this tool allows you to quickly set a material at a specific index as the active one.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAdd HDRI Light:\u003c/strong\u003e Prompts for an HDRI image file and sets it up as the world lighting, providing realistic illumination for your scene.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eApply All Modifiers:\u003c/strong\u003e Iterates through all mesh objects in the scene, applies their modifier stacks, and converts geometry instances (like particle systems or collection instances) into real mesh data. This helps prepare models for texturing.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eConvert Curves to Mesh:\u003c/strong\u003e Converts any selected curve objects into mesh objects, which is necessary before StableGen can texture them.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExport  GIF/MP4:\u003c/strong\u003e Creates an animated GIF and MP4 video of the currently active object, with the camera ing around it. Useful for quickly showcasing your textured model. You can set duration, frame rate, and resolution.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReproject Images:\u003c/strong\u003e This operator re-applies previously generated textures to your models using the latest \u003ccode\u003eViewpoint Blending Settings\u003c/code\u003e (e.g., \u003ccode\u003eDiscard-Over Angle\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eWeight Exponent\u003c/code\u003e). This allows you to tweak texture blending without full regeneration.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eExperiment with these settings and tools to achieve a vast range of effects and control! Remember that the optimal parameters can vary greatly depending on the model, subject matter, and desired artistic style.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e Output Directory Structure\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content--output-directory-structure\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink:  Output Directory Structure\" href=\"#-output-directory-structure\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eStableGen organizes the generated files within the \u003ccode\u003eOutput Directory\u003c/code\u003e specified in your addon preferences. For each generation session, a new timestamped folder is created, helping you keep track of different iterations. The structure for each session (revision) is as follows:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;Output Directory\u0026gt;/\u003c/code\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;SceneName\u0026gt;/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Based on your \u003ccode\u003e.blend\u003c/code\u003e file name, or scene name if unsaved)\u003c/em\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;YYYY-MM-DDTHH-MM-SS\u0026gt;/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Timestamp of generation start - this is the main revision directory)\u003c/em\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003egenerated/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Main output textures from each camera/viewpoint before being applied or baked)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econtrolnet/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Intermediate ControlNet input images)\u003c/em\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edepth/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Depth pass renders)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecanny/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Renders processed using Canny edge decetor)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003enormal/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Normal pass renders)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebaked/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Textures baked onto UV maps using the standalone \u003ccode\u003eBake Textures\u003c/code\u003e tool)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003egenerated_baked/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Textures baked as part of the generation process if \"Bake Textures While Generating\" is enabled)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003einpaint/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Files related to inpainting processes, e.g., for \u003ccode\u003eSequential mode\u003c/code\u003e)\u003c/em\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003erender/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Renders of previous state used as context for inpainting)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003evisibility/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Visibility masks used as masks during the inpainting)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003euv_inpaint/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Files specific to the UV Inpaint mode)\u003c/em\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003euv_visibility/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Visibility masks generated on UVs for UV inpainting)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emisc/\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(Other temporary or miscellaneous files, e.g., renders made for Canny edge detection input)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e.gif\u003c/code\u003e / \u003ccode\u003e.mp4\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(If the \u003ccode\u003eExport  GIF/MP4\u003c/code\u003e tool is used, these files are saved directly into the timestamped revision directory)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eprompt.json\u003c/code\u003e \u003cem\u003e(The last generated workflow to be used in ComfyUI)\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEncountering issues? Here are some common fixes. Always check the \u003cstrong\u003eBlender System Console\u003c/strong\u003e (Window \u0026gt; Toggle System Console) AND the \u003cstrong\u003eComfyUI server console\u003c/strong\u003e for error messages.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eStableGen Panel Not Showing:\u003c/strong\u003e Ensure the addon is installed and enabled in Blender's preferences.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\"Cannot generate...\" on Generate Button:\u003c/strong\u003e Check Addon Preferences: \u003ccode\u003eModel Directory\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eOutput Directory\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003eServer Address\u003c/code\u003e must be correctly set.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eConnection Issues with ComfyUI:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMake sure your ComfyUI server is running.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eVerify the \u003ccode\u003eServer Address\u003c/code\u003e in StableGen preferences.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCheck firewall settings.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eModels Not Found (Error in ComfyUI Console):\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRun the \u003ccode\u003einstaller.py\u003c/code\u003e script.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eManually ensure models are in the correct subfolders of \u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;YourComfyUIDirectory\u0026gt;/models/\u003c/code\u003e (e.g., \u003ccode\u003echeckpoints/\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003econtrolnet/\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eloras/\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eipadapter/\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eclip_vision/\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eRestart ComfyUI after adding new models or custom nodes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGPU Out Of Memory (OOM):\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEnable \u003ccode\u003eAuto Rescale Resolution\u003c/code\u003e in \u003ccode\u003eAdvanced Parameters\u003c/code\u003e \u0026gt; \u003ccode\u003eOutput \u0026amp; Material Settings\u003c/code\u003e if disabled.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTry lower bake resolutions if baking.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eClose other GPU-intensive applications.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTextures not visible after generation completes:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSwitch to Rendered viewport shading (top right corner, fourth \"sphere\" icon)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTextures not affected by your lighting setup:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEnable \u003ccode\u003eApply BSDF\u003c/code\u003e in \u003ccode\u003eAdvanced Parameters \u0026gt; Output \u0026amp; Material Settings\u003c/code\u003e and regenerate.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePoor Texture Quality/Artifacts:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTry using the provided presets.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAdjust prompts and negative prompts.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eExperiment with different Generation Modes. \u003ccode\u003eSequential\u003c/code\u003e with IPAdapter is often good for consistency.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEnsure adequate camera coverage and appropriate \u003ccode\u003eDiscard-Over Angle\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFine-tune ControlNet strength. Too low might ignore geometry; too high might yield flat results.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFor \u003ccode\u003eSequential\u003c/code\u003e mode, check inpainting and visibility mask settings.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAll Visible Meshes Textured:\u003c/strong\u003e StableGen textures all visible mesh objects by default. You can set \u003ccode\u003eTarget Objects\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003eSelected\u003c/code\u003e to only texture selected objects.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e Contributing\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content--contributing\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink:  Contributing\" href=\"#-contributing\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWe welcome contributions! Radek Richtr, Ph.D.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCore Technologies \u0026amp; Communities:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eComfyUI\u003c/strong\u003e by ComfyAnonymous (\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/comfyanonymous/ComfyUI\"\u003eGitHub\u003c/a\u003e) for the powerful and flexible backend.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eThe \u003cstrong\u003eBlender Foundation\u003c/strong\u003e and its community for the amazing open-source 3D creation suite.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eInspired by following Blender Addons:\u003c/strong\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDream Textures\u003c/strong\u003e by Carson Katri et al. 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eHere are some features we plan to implement in the future (in no particular order):\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAdvanced IPAdapter support:\u003c/strong\u003e Support for custom IPAdapter models, support for advanced IPAdapter parameters.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUpscaling:\u003c/strong\u003e Support for upscaling generated textures.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFLUX.1-dev hycJXc"><section aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 fGqKFv"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eoaCFS js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned undefined" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">StableGen: AI-Powered 3D Texturing in Blender </h1><a id="user-content-stablegen-ai-powered-3d-texturing-in-blender-" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: StableGen: AI-Powered 3D Texturing in Blender " href="#stablegen-ai-powered-3d-texturing-in-blender-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.gnu.org/licenses/gpl-3.0" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/8a398fc9fbf479a323d2d91b9fcb6fb9c6b4d08e96dbb544488ccbed312115fc/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f4c6963656e73652d47504c76332d626c75652e737667" alt="License: GPL v3" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/License-GPLv3-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="#system-requirements"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/307752b7e5cca93d8a1a724fe0ff6c99e3ed7ee34c6ffc55bf8ef99b1071e603/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f426c656e6465722d342e322532422d6f72616e67652e737667" alt="Blender Version" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Blender-4.2%2B-orange.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Transform your 3D texturing workflow with the power of generative AI, directly within Blender!</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">StableGen is an open-source Blender plugin designed to seamlessly integrate advanced diffusion models (SDXL, FLUX.1-dev) into your creative process. Generate complex, coherent, and controllable textures for your 3D models and entire scenes using a flexible ComfyUI backend.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> Key Features</h2><a id="user-content--key-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  Key Features" href="#-key-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">StableGen empowers 3D artists by bringing cutting-edge AI texturing capabilities into Blender:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li> <strong>Scene-Wide Multi-Mesh Texturing:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Don't just texture one mesh at a time! StableGen is designed to apply textures to <strong>all mesh objects in your scene simultaneously</strong> from your defined camera viewpoints. Alternatively, you can choose to texture only selected objects.</li>
<li>Achieve a cohesive look across entire environments or collections of assets in a single generation pass.</li>
<li>Ideal for concept art, look development for complex scenes, and batch-texturing asset libraries.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li> <strong>Multi-View Consistency:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Sequential Mode:</strong> Generates textures viewpoint by viewpoint on each mesh, using inpainting and visibility masks for high consistency across complex surfaces.</li>
<li><strong>Grid Mode:</strong> Processes multiple viewpoints for all meshes simultaneously for faster previews. Includes an optional refinement pass.</li>
<li>Sophisticated weighted blending ensures smooth transitions between views.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li> <strong>Precise Geometric Control with ControlNet:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Leverage multiple ControlNet units (Depth, Canny, Normal) simultaneously to ensure generated textures respect your model's geometry.</li>
<li>Fine-tune strength, start/end steps for each ControlNet unit.</li>
<li>Supports custom ControlNet model mapping.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>锔 <strong>Powerful Style Guidance with IPAdapter:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use external reference images to guide the style, mood, and content of your textures with IPAdapter.</li>
<li>Employ IPAdapter without an reference image for enhanced consistency in multi-view generation modes.</li>
<li>Control IPAdapter strength, weight type, and active steps.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>锔 <strong>Flexible ComfyUI Backend:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Connects to your existing ComfyUI installation, allowing you to use your preferred SDXL checkpoints and custom LoRAs. Experimental support for FLUX.1-dev.</li>
<li>Offloads heavy computation to the ComfyUI server, keeping Blender mostly responsive.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li> <strong>Advanced Inpainting &amp; Refinement:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Refine Mode (Img2Img):</strong> Re-style, enhance, or add detail to existing textures (StableGen generated or otherwise) using an image-to-image process. Choose to preserve original textures for localized refinement.</li>
<li><strong>UV Inpaint Mode:</strong> Intelligently fills untextured areas directly on your model's UV map using surrounding texture context.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>锔 <strong>Integrated Workflow Tools:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Camera Setup:</strong> Quickly add and arrange multiple cameras around your subject.</li>
<li><strong>View-Specific Prompts:</strong> Assign unique text prompts to individual camera viewpoints for targeted details.</li>
<li><strong>Texture Baking:</strong> Convert complex procedural StableGen materials into standard UV image textures.</li>
<li><strong>HDRI Setup, Modifier Application, Curve Conversion, GIF/MP4 Export &amp; Reproject.</strong></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li> <strong>Preset System:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Get started quickly with built-in presets for common scenarios (e.g., "Default", "Characters", "Quick Draft").</li>
<li>Save and manage your own custom parameter configurations for repeatable workflows.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<hr>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">锔 How It Works (A Glimpse)</h2><a id="user-content-锔-how-it-works-a-glimpse" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 锔 How It Works (A Glimpse)" href="#锔-how-it-works-a-glimpse"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">StableGen acts as an intuitive interface within Blender that communicates with a ComfyUI backend.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>You set up your scene and parameters in the StableGen panel.</li>
<li>StableGen prepares necessary data (like ControlNet inputs from camera views).</li>
<li>It constructs a workflow and sends it to your ComfyUI server.</li>
<li>ComfyUI processes the request using your selected diffusion models.</li>
<li>Generated images are sent back to Blender.</li>
<li>StableGen applies these images as textures to your models using sophisticated projection and blending techniques.</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> System Requirements</h2><a id="user-content--system-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  System Requirements" href="#-system-requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Blender:</strong> Version 4.2 or newer.</li>
<li><strong>Operating System:</strong> Windows 10/11 or Linux.</li>
<li><strong>GPU:</strong> <strong>NVIDIA GPU with CUDA is recommended</strong> for ComfyUI. For further details, check ComfyUI's github page: <a href="https://github.com/comfyanonymous/ComfyUI">https://github.com/comfyanonymous/ComfyUI</a>.</li>
<li><strong>ComfyUI:</strong> A working installation of ComfyUI. StableGen uses this as its backend.</li>
<li><strong>Python:</strong> Version 3.x (usually comes with Blender, but Python 3 is needed for the <code>installer.py</code> script).</li>
<li><strong>Git:</strong> Required by the <code>installer.py</code> script.</li>
<li><strong>Disk Space:</strong> Significant free space for ComfyUI, AI models (10GB to 50GB+), and generated textures.</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">锔 Installation</h2><a id="user-content-锔-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 锔 Installation" href="#锔-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Setting up StableGen involves installing ComfyUI, then StableGen's dependencies into ComfyUI using our installer script, and finally installing the StableGen plugin in Blender.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 1: Install ComfyUI (If not already installed)</h3><a id="user-content-step-1-install-comfyui-if-not-already-installed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 1: Install ComfyUI (If not already installed)" href="#step-1-install-comfyui-if-not-already-installed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">StableGen relies on a working ComfyUI installation as its backend.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>If you don't have ComfyUI, please follow the <strong>official ComfyUI installation guide</strong>: <a href="https://github.com/comfyanonymous/ComfyUI#installing">https://github.com/comfyanonymous/ComfyUI#installing</a>.
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Install ComfyUI in a dedicated directory. We'll refer to this as <code>&lt;YourComfyUIDirectory&gt;</code>.</li>
<li>Ensure you can run ComfyUI and it's functioning correctly before proceeding.</li>
<li>Remote ComfyUI instances are not currently supported. This includes ComfyUI installations running on a different machine or in a virtual machine (including WSL).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 2: Install Dependencies (Custom Nodes &amp; AI Models) - Automated (Recommended)</h3><a id="user-content-step-2-install-dependencies-custom-nodes--ai-models---automated-recommended" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 2: Install Dependencies (Custom Nodes &amp; AI Models) - Automated (Recommended)" href="#step-2-install-dependencies-custom-nodes--ai-models---automated-recommended"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>installer.py</code> script (found in this repository) automates the download and placement of required ComfyUI custom nodes and core AI models into your <code>&lt;YourComfyUIDirectory&gt;</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Prerequisites for the installer:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Python 3.</li>
<li>Git installed and accessible in your system's PATH.</li>
<li>The path to your ComfyUI installation (<code>&lt;YourComfyUIDirectory&gt;</code>).</li>
<li>Required Python packages for the script: <code>requests</code> and <code>tqdm</code>. Install them via pip:
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pip install requests tqdm"><pre>pip install requests tqdm</pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Running the Installer:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Download/Locate the Installer:</strong> Get <code>installer.py</code> from this GitHub repository.</li>
<li><strong>Execute the Script:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Open your system's terminal or command prompt.</li>
<li>Navigate to the directory containing <code>installer.py</code>.</li>
<li>Run the script:
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python installer.py &lt;YourComfyUIDirectory&gt;"><pre>python installer.py <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>YourComfyUIDirectory<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span></pre></div>
Replace <code>&lt;YourComfyUIDirectory&gt;</code> with the actual path. If omitted, the script will prompt for it.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Follow On-Screen Instructions:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The script will display a menu of installation packages (Minimal, Essential, Recommended, Complete SDXL). Choose one based on your needs.</li>
<li>It will download and place files into the correct subdirectories of <code>&lt;YourComfyUIDirectory&gt;</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Restart ComfyUI:</strong> If ComfyUI was running, restart it to load new custom nodes.</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><em>(For manual dependency installation (and for installation of FLUX.1-dev and its dependecies), see <code>docs/MANUAL_INSTALLATION.md</code>.)</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 3: Install StableGen Blender Plugin</h3><a id="user-content-step-3-install-stablegen-blender-plugin" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 3: Install StableGen Blender Plugin" href="#step-3-install-stablegen-blender-plugin"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Go to the <a href="https://github.com/sakalond/stablegen/releases"><strong>Releases</strong> page</a> of this repository.</li>
<li>Download the latest <code>StableGen.zip</code> file.</li>
<li>In Blender, go to <code>Edit &gt; Preferences &gt; Add-ons &gt; Install...</code>.</li>
<li>Navigate to and select the downloaded <code>StableGen.zip</code> file.</li>
<li>Enable the "StableGen" addon (search for "StableGen" and check the box).</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 4: Configure StableGen Plugin in Blender</h3><a id="user-content-step-4-configure-stablegen-plugin-in-blender" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 4: Configure StableGen Plugin in Blender" href="#step-4-configure-stablegen-plugin-in-blender"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>In Blender, go to <code>Edit &gt; Preferences &gt; Add-ons</code>.</li>
<li>Find "StableGen" and expand its preferences.</li>
<li>Set the following paths:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>ComfyUI Directory:</strong> Path to your ComfyUI installation (e.g., <code>&lt;YourComfyUIDirectory&gt;</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Output Directory:</strong> Choose a folder where StableGen will save generated images.</li>
<li><strong>Server Address:</strong> Ensure this matches your ComfyUI server (default <code>127.0.0.1:8188</code>).</li>
<li>Review <strong>ControlNet Mapping</strong> if using custom named ControlNet models.</li>
<li><strong>External Checkpoints / LoRAs Directory (Optional):</strong> Path to your external checkpoint directory. Also has to be configured in ComfyUI.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Enable online access in Blender if not enabled already. Select <code>Edit -&gt; Preferences</code> from the topbar of Blender. Then navigate to <code>System -&gt; Network</code> and check the box <code>Enable Online Access</code>. While StableGen does not require internet access, this is added to respect Blender add-on guidelines, as there are still network calls being made locally.</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> Quick Start Guide</h2><a id="user-content--quick-start-guide" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  Quick Start Guide" href="#-quick-start-guide"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Heres how to get your first texture generated with StableGen:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Start ComfyUI Server:</strong> Make sure it's running in the background.</li>
<li><strong>Open Blender &amp; Prepare Scene:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Have a mesh object ready (e.g., the default Cube).</li>
<li>Ensure the StableGen addon is enabled and configured (see Step 4 above).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Access StableGen Panel:</strong> Press <code>N</code> in the 3D Viewport, go to the "StableGen" tab.</li>
<li><strong>Add Cameras (Recommended for Multi-View):</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Select your object.</li>
<li>In the StableGen panel, click "<strong>Add Cameras</strong>". Choose <code>Object</code> as center type. Adjust interactively if needed, then confirm.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Set Basic Parameters:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Prompt:</strong> Type a description (e.g., "ancient stone wall with moss").</li>
<li><strong>Checkpoint:</strong> Select a checkpoint (e.g., <code>sdxl_base_1.0</code>).</li>
<li><strong>Generation Mode:</strong> <code>Sequential</code> is a good starting point for consistency.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Hit Generate!</strong> Click the main "<strong>Generate</strong>" button.</li>
<li><strong>Observe:</strong> Watch the progress in the panel and the ComfyUI console. Your object should update with the new texture! Output files will be in your specified "Output Directory".
<ul dir="auto">
<li>By default, the generated texture will only be visible in the Rendered viewport shading mode (CYCLES Render Engine).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> Usage &amp; Parameters Overview</h2><a id="user-content--usage--parameters-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  Usage &amp; Parameters Overview" href="#-usage--parameters-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">StableGen provides a comprehensive interface for controlling your AI texturing process, from initial setup to final output. Here's an overview of the main sections and tools available in the StableGen panel:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Primary Actions &amp; Scene Setup</h3><a id="user-content-primary-actions--scene-setup" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Primary Actions &amp; Scene Setup" href="#primary-actions--scene-setup"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These are the main operational buttons and initial setup tools, generally found near the top of the StableGen panel:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Generate / Cancel Generation (Main Button):</strong> This is the primary button to start the AI texture generation process for meshe objects based on your current settings. It communicates with the ComfyUI backend. While processing, the button changes to "Cancel Generation," allowing you to stop the current task. Progress bars will appear below this button during generation.</li>
<li><strong>Bake Textures:</strong> Converts the dynamic, multi-projection material StableGen creates on your meshes into a single, standard UV-mapped image texture per object. This is essential for exporting or simplifying scenes. You can set the resolution and UV unwrapping method for the bake. This option is crucial for finalizing your AI-generated textures into a portable format.</li>
<li><strong>Add Cameras:</strong> Helps you quickly set up multiple viewpoints. It creates a circular array of Blender cameras around the active object (if "Object" center type is chosen) or the current 3D view center. You can specify the number of cameras and interactively adjust their positions before finalizing.</li>
<li><strong>Collect Camera Prompts:</strong> Cycles through all cameras in your scene, allowing you to type a specific descriptive text prompt for each viewpoint (e.g., "front view," "close-up on face"). These per-camera prompts are used in conjunction with the main prompt if <code>Use camera prompts</code> is enabled in <code>Viewpoint Blending Settings</code>.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Preset Management</h3><a id="user-content-preset-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Preset Management" href="#preset-management"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Located prominently in the UI, this system allows you to:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Select a Preset:</strong> Choose from built-in configurations (e.g., <code>Default</code>, <code>Characters</code>, <code>Quick Draft</code>) for common scenarios or select <code>Custom</code> to use your current settings.</li>
<li><strong>Apply Preset:</strong> If you modify a stock preset, this button applies its original values.</li>
<li><strong>Save Preset:</strong> When your settings are <code>Custom</code>, this allows you to save your current configuration as a new named preset.</li>
<li><strong>Delete Preset:</strong> Removes a selected custom preset.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Main Parameters</h3><a id="user-content-main-parameters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Main Parameters" href="#main-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These are your primary controls for defining the generation:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Prompt:</strong> The main text description of the texture you want to generate.</li>
<li><strong>Checkpoint:</strong> Select the base SDXL checkpoint.</li>
<li><strong>Architecture:</strong> Choose between <code>SDXL</code> and <code>Flux 1</code> (experimental) model architectures.</li>
<li><strong>Generation Mode:</strong> Defines the core strategy for texturing:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Generate Separately</code>: Each viewpoint generates independently.</li>
<li><code>Generate Sequentially</code>: Viewpoints generate one by one, using inpainting from previous views for consistency.</li>
<li><code>Generate Using Grid</code>: Combines all views into a grid for a single generation pass, with an optional refinement step.</li>
<li><code>Refine/Restyle Texture (Img2Img)</code>: Uses the current texture as input for an image-to-image process.</li>
<li><code>UV Inpaint Missing Areas</code>: Fills untextured areas on a UV map via inpainting.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Target Objects:</strong> Choose whether to texture all visible mesh objects or only selected ones.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Advanced Parameters (Collapsible Sections)</h3><a id="user-content-advanced-parameters-collapsible-sections" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Advanced Parameters (Collapsible Sections)" href="#advanced-parameters-collapsible-sections"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Click the arrow next to each title to expand and access detailed settings:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Core Generation Settings:</strong> Control diffusion basics like Seed, Steps, CFG, Negative Prompt, Sampler, Scheduler and Clip Skip.</li>
<li><strong>LoRA Management:</strong> Add and configure LoRAs (Low-Rank Adaptation) for additional style or content guidance. You can set the model and clip strength for each LoRA.</li>
<li><strong>Viewpoint Blending Settings:</strong> Manage how textures from different camera views are combined, including camera-specific prompts, discard angles, and blending weight exponents.</li>
<li><strong>Output &amp; Material Settings:</strong> Define fallback color, material properties (BSDF), automatic resolution scaling, and options for baking textures during generation which enables generating with more than 8 viewpoints.</li>
<li><strong>Image Guidance (IPAdapter &amp; ControlNet):</strong> Configure IPAdapter for style transfer using external images and set up multiple ControlNet units (Depth, Canny, etc.) for precise structural control.</li>
<li><strong>Inpainting Options:</strong> Fine-tune masking and blending for <code>Sequential</code> and <code>UV Inpaint</code> modes (e.g., differential diffusion, mask blurring/growing).</li>
<li><strong>Generation Mode Specifics:</strong> Parameters unique to the selected Generation Mode, like refinement options for Grid mode or IPAdapter consistency settings for Sequential/Separate/Refine modes.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Integrated Workflow Tools (Bottom Section)</h3><a id="user-content-integrated-workflow-tools-bottom-section" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Integrated Workflow Tools (Bottom Section)" href="#integrated-workflow-tools-bottom-section"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A collection of utilities to further support your texturing workflow:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Switch Material:</strong> For selected objects with multiple material slots, this tool allows you to quickly set a material at a specific index as the active one.</li>
<li><strong>Add HDRI Light:</strong> Prompts for an HDRI image file and sets it up as the world lighting, providing realistic illumination for your scene.</li>
<li><strong>Apply All Modifiers:</strong> Iterates through all mesh objects in the scene, applies their modifier stacks, and converts geometry instances (like particle systems or collection instances) into real mesh data. This helps prepare models for texturing.</li>
<li><strong>Convert Curves to Mesh:</strong> Converts any selected curve objects into mesh objects, which is necessary before StableGen can texture them.</li>
<li><strong>Export  GIF/MP4:</strong> Creates an animated GIF and MP4 video of the currently active object, with the camera ing around it. Useful for quickly showcasing your textured model. You can set duration, frame rate, and resolution.</li>
<li><strong>Reproject Images:</strong> This operator re-applies previously generated textures to your models using the latest <code>Viewpoint Blending Settings</code> (e.g., <code>Discard-Over Angle</code>, <code>Weight Exponent</code>). This allows you to tweak texture blending without full regeneration.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Experiment with these settings and tools to achieve a vast range of effects and control! Remember that the optimal parameters can vary greatly depending on the model, subject matter, and desired artistic style.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> Output Directory Structure</h2><a id="user-content--output-directory-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  Output Directory Structure" href="#-output-directory-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">StableGen organizes the generated files within the <code>Output Directory</code> specified in your addon preferences. For each generation session, a new timestamped folder is created, helping you keep track of different iterations. The structure for each session (revision) is as follows:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>&lt;Output Directory&gt;/</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>&lt;SceneName&gt;/</code> <em>(Based on your <code>.blend</code> file name, or scene name if unsaved)</em>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>&lt;YYYY-MM-DDTHH-MM-SS&gt;/</code> <em>(Timestamp of generation start - this is the main revision directory)</em>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>generated/</code> <em>(Main output textures from each camera/viewpoint before being applied or baked)</em></li>
<li><code>controlnet/</code> <em>(Intermediate ControlNet input images)</em>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>depth/</code> <em>(Depth pass renders)</em></li>
<li><code>canny/</code> <em>(Renders processed using Canny edge decetor)</em></li>
<li><code>normal/</code> <em>(Normal pass renders)</em></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>baked/</code> <em>(Textures baked onto UV maps using the standalone <code>Bake Textures</code> tool)</em></li>
<li><code>generated_baked/</code> <em>(Textures baked as part of the generation process if "Bake Textures While Generating" is enabled)</em></li>
<li><code>inpaint/</code> <em>(Files related to inpainting processes, e.g., for <code>Sequential mode</code>)</em>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>render/</code> <em>(Renders of previous state used as context for inpainting)</em></li>
<li><code>visibility/</code> <em>(Visibility masks used as masks during the inpainting)</em></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>uv_inpaint/</code> <em>(Files specific to the UV Inpaint mode)</em>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>uv_visibility/</code> <em>(Visibility masks generated on UVs for UV inpainting)</em></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>misc/</code> <em>(Other temporary or miscellaneous files, e.g., renders made for Canny edge detection input)</em></li>
<li><code>.gif</code> / <code>.mp4</code> <em>(If the <code>Export  GIF/MP4</code> tool is used, these files are saved directly into the timestamped revision directory)</em></li>
<li><code>prompt.json</code> <em>(The last generated workflow to be used in ComfyUI)</em></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> Troubleshooting</h2><a id="user-content--troubleshooting" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  Troubleshooting" href="#-troubleshooting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Encountering issues? Here are some common fixes. Always check the <strong>Blender System Console</strong> (Window &gt; Toggle System Console) AND the <strong>ComfyUI server console</strong> for error messages.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>StableGen Panel Not Showing:</strong> Ensure the addon is installed and enabled in Blender's preferences.</li>
<li><strong>"Cannot generate..." on Generate Button:</strong> Check Addon Preferences: <code>Model Directory</code>, <code>Output Directory</code>, and <code>Server Address</code> must be correctly set.</li>
<li><strong>Connection Issues with ComfyUI:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Make sure your ComfyUI server is running.</li>
<li>Verify the <code>Server Address</code> in StableGen preferences.</li>
<li>Check firewall settings.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Models Not Found (Error in ComfyUI Console):</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Run the <code>installer.py</code> script.</li>
<li>Manually ensure models are in the correct subfolders of <code>&lt;YourComfyUIDirectory&gt;/models/</code> (e.g., <code>checkpoints/</code>, <code>controlnet/</code>, <code>loras/</code>, <code>ipadapter/</code>, <code>clip_vision/</code>).</li>
<li>Restart ComfyUI after adding new models or custom nodes.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>GPU Out Of Memory (OOM):</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Enable <code>Auto Rescale Resolution</code> in <code>Advanced Parameters</code> &gt; <code>Output &amp; Material Settings</code> if disabled.</li>
<li>Try lower bake resolutions if baking.</li>
<li>Close other GPU-intensive applications.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Textures not visible after generation completes:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Switch to Rendered viewport shading (top right corner, fourth "sphere" icon)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Textures not affected by your lighting setup:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Enable <code>Apply BSDF</code> in <code>Advanced Parameters &gt; Output &amp; Material Settings</code> and regenerate.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Poor Texture Quality/Artifacts:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Try using the provided presets.</li>
<li>Adjust prompts and negative prompts.</li>
<li>Experiment with different Generation Modes. <code>Sequential</code> with IPAdapter is often good for consistency.</li>
<li>Ensure adequate camera coverage and appropriate <code>Discard-Over Angle</code>.</li>
<li>Fine-tune ControlNet strength. Too low might ignore geometry; too high might yield flat results.</li>
<li>For <code>Sequential</code> mode, check inpainting and visibility mask settings.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>All Visible Meshes Textured:</strong> StableGen textures all visible mesh objects by default. You can set <code>Target Objects</code> to <code>Selected</code> to only texture selected objects.</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> Contributing</h2><a id="user-content--contributing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  Contributing" href="#-contributing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We welcome contributions! Whether it's bug reports, feature suggestions, code contributions, or new presets, please feel free to open an issue or a pull request.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> License</h2><a id="user-content--license" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  License" href="#-license"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
