<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> Acknowledgements</h2><a id="user-content--acknowledgements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  Acknowledgements" href="#-acknowledgements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">StableGen builds upon the fantastic work of many individuals and communities. Our sincere thanks go to:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Academic Roots:</strong> This plugin originated as a Bachelor's Thesis by Ondej Sakala at the Czech Technical University in Prague (Faculty of Information Technology), supervised by Ing. Radek Richtr, Ph.D.</li>
<li><strong>Core Technologies &amp; Communities:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>ComfyUI</strong> by ComfyAnonymous (<a href="https://github.com/comfyanonymous/ComfyUI">GitHub</a>) for the powerful and flexible backend.</li>
<li>The <strong>Blender Foundation</strong> and its community for the amazing open-source 3D creation suite.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Inspired by following Blender Addons:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Dream Textures</strong> by Carson Katri et al. (<a href="https://github.com/carson-katri/dream-textures">GitHub</a>)</li>
<li><strong>Diffused Texture Addon</strong> by Frederik Hasecke (<a href="https://github.com/FrederikHasecke/diffused-texture-addon">GitHub</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Pioneering Research:</strong> We are indebted to the researchers behind key advancements that power StableGen. The following list highlights some of the foundational and influential works in diffusion models, AI-driven control, and 3D texturing (links to arXiv pre-prints):
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Diffusion Models:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Ho et al. (2020), Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Models - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2006.11239" rel="nofollow">2006.11239</a></li>
<li>Rombach et al. (2022), Latent Diffusion Models (Stable Diffusion) - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2112.10752" rel="nofollow">2112.10752</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>AI Control Mechanisms:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Zhang et al. (2023), ControlNet - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2302.05543" rel="nofollow">2302.05543</a></li>
<li>Ye et al. (2023), IP-Adapter - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2308.06721" rel="nofollow">2308.06721</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Key 3D Texture Synthesis Papers:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Chen et al. (2023), Text2Tex - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2303.11396" rel="nofollow">2303.11396</a></li>
<li>Richardson et al. (2023), TEXTure - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2302.01721" rel="nofollow">2302.01721</a></li>
<li>Zeng et al. (2023), Paint3D - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2312.13913" rel="nofollow">2312.13913</a></li>
<li>Le et al. (2024), EucliDreamer - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2311.15573" rel="nofollow">2311.15573</a></li>
<li>Ceylan et al. (2024), MatAtlas - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2404.02899" rel="nofollow">2404.02899</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Other Influential Works:</strong>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Siddiqui et al. (2022), Texturify - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2204.02411" rel="nofollow">2204.02411</a></li>
<li>Bokhovkin et al. (2023), Mesh2Tex - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2304.05868" rel="nofollow">2304.05868</a></li>
<li>Levin &amp; Fried (2024), Differential Diffusion - <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2306.00950" rel="nofollow">2306.00950</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">The open spirit of the AI and open-source communities is what makes projects like StableGen possible.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"> List of planned features</h2><a id="user-content--list-of-planned-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  List of planned features" href="#-list-of-planned-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Here are some features we plan to implement in the future (in no particular order):</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Advanced IPAdapter support:</strong> Support for custom IPAdapter models, support for advanced IPAdapter parameters.</li>
<li><strong>Upscaling:</strong> Support for upscaling generated textures.</li>
<li><strong>FLUX.1-dev Support:</strong> Full support for the FLUX.1-dev, including IPAdapter, depth control LoRAs, and more.</li>
<li><strong>SD 3.5 Support:</strong> Support for the Stable Diffusion 3.5 architecture.</li>
<li><strong>Remote ComfyUI Support:</strong> Allow connecting to remote ComfyUI servers, enabling distributed processing.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">If you have any suggestions, please feel free to open an issue!</p>
<hr>
